If the joint type is Aligned, the target structure will be placed such that the rotation of the target Jigsaw Block aligns with the rotation of the source Jigsaw Block. If the joint type is Aligned, the target structure will be placed such that the rotation of the target Jigsaw Block aligns with the rotation of the source Jigsaw Block. При выровненном типе строение будет расположено так, что прокрутка целевого блога-фрагмента будет связана с прокруткой исходного. If the joint type is Aligned, the target structure will be placed such that the rotation of the target Jigsaw Block aligns with the rotation of the source Jigsaw Block. Note that this only applies when the Jigsaw Block is placed facing up or down.".

If the joint type is Aligned, the target structure will be placed such that the rotation of the target Jigsaw Block aligns with the rotation of the source Jigsaw Block. Pieces will be processed in descending priority with insertion order breaking ties.".

If the joint type is Rollable, the target structure will be rotated randomly around the source Jigsaw Block. If the joint type is Aligned, the target structure will be placed such that the rotation of the target Jigsaw Block aligns with the rotation of the source Jigsaw Block. Note that this only applies when the Jigsaw Block is placed facing up or down.".
